6/21/25, 11:53â€¯PM - +92 310 6387577: As a developer, you know the hassle of reinstalling Windows and then having to reinstall all your development tools and software, like Red Panda C++, VSCode, Python, Java, etc. Is there a way to bundle your development environment with the Windows installation? In Linux, this is achievable by creating a custom distro. You can install a base Linux distro, add all the software you need, and then create an ISO file or a bootable USB drive. Can something similar be done with Windows?

It is difficult in windows as compare to linux butmight want to explore options like:

1. *Windows Answer File*: An XML file that automates Windows installation and configuration.
2. *Windows Deployment Services*: A role service that allows you to deploy Windows images.
3. *Chocolatey*: A package manager for Windows that can automate software installation.
4. *Custom Windows images*: You can create a custom Windows image with pre-installed software using tools like DISM (Deployment Image Servicing and Management).
